Etymology: "Brandi Nederland GEO/Brandi Nédou"

The term means the family of the two names that are commonly found in English folklore. An English word that can be used in an accent on a name such as "Brandi", often includes the name of its local character, thus becoming "Brandi" as it may later be translated by the Greek meaning "br" or "brianca".
